war_with_soviets = {
	allowed = {
		tag = POL
	}
	enable = {
		country_exists = DNZ
		DNZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	
	ai_strategy = {
		type = protect
		id = "DNZ"			
		value = 100
	}
}

protect_danzig_against_germany = {
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			tag = FRA
			tag = ENG
		}
	}
	enable = {
		OR = {
			tag = FRA
			tag = ENG
		}
		GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_end_of_czechoslovakia }
		GER = { NOT = { has_war_with = DNZ } }
		country_exists = DNZ
	}
	abort = {
		NOT = { country_exists = DNZ }
	}
	
	ai_strategy = {
		type = protect
		id = "DNZ"			
		value = 200
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = diplo_action_desire
		id = DNZ
		target = guarantee
		value = 20
	}
}
